## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in grafana/grafana that implement configuration loading: the INI file parser, the environment variable override logic, the default values per section, and the sensitive config value masking for the /api/admin/settings endpoint.

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the platform domain.

   - `RedactedURL()` - masks passwords in URLs

   - `LogConfigSources()` - logs config sources
   - `Load()` - main entry point
   - `NewCfg()`, `NewCfgFromArgs()`, `NewCfgFromBytes()`, `NewCfgFromINIFile()` - constructors

   - `fileExpander` - expands $__file{path} references

   - `Provider` interface

   - `Current()` - returns current settings with redacted values

## Grafana Config System — Complete Source File Map

### 1. INI File Parsing

**Primary file:** `pkg/setting/setting.go`

The entire config system is built on `gopkg.in/ini.v1`. The load chain is:

| Function | Line | Role |
|---|---|---|
| `loadConfiguration()` | 963 | Orchestrates the full load: reads `conf/defaults.ini` via `ini.Load()`, applies CLI defaults, loads `custom.ini`, applies env overrides, applies CLI overrides, expands variable references |
| `loadSpecifiedConfigFile()` | 922 | Loads `custom.ini` (or `--config` path) via `ini.Load()` and merges every section/key into the master `*ini.File`, overwriting defaults |
| `parseINIFile()` | 1165 | Receives the fully-merged `*ini.File`, stores it as `cfg.Raw`, then dispatches to all ~30 `readXxx` section readers |
| `NewCfgFromBytes()` | 1100 | Parses raw `[]byte` as INI via `ini.Load()` |
| `NewCfgFromINIFile()` | 1116 | Accepts an already-parsed `*ini.File`, skips the load chain |
| `valueAsString()` | 1453 | Thin wrapper around `section.Key(k).MustString(default)` — the universal default-value helper |

**Default values file:** `conf/defaults.ini` — loaded first; every key in it becomes the baseline that custom config and env vars override.

---

### 2. Environment Variable Override Logic

**Primary files:** `pkg/setting/setting.go`, `pkg/setting/expanders.go`

**Batch override at load time** (`setting.go`):
- `EnvKey(section, key)` (L855) — converts `[auth.saml]` + `enabled` → `GF_AUTH_SAML_ENABLED` (dots/hyphens → underscores, uppercased)
- `applyEnvVariableOverrides()` (L744) — iterates every section/key in the parsed file, calls `EnvKey()`, reads `os.Getenv()`, calls `k
... (truncated)
